### [37] [Data-Efficient Domain Adaptation for LLM-based MT using Contrastive Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27556)
*Inacio Vieira,Antonio Castaldo,James O'Doherty,Sheila Castilho*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种数据高效的领域自适应方法，通过使用 CPO（Conditional Preference Optimization）来模拟机器翻译（MT）的后编辑工作流。该方法通过将基础模型的原始输出视为“拒绝”样本，将人类批准的翻译记忆库（TM）条目视为“选择”样本，合成了偏好对。实验表明，仅使用 14.7k 个偏好对，该模型在英-巴西葡语和英-韩语翻译任务上取得了接近使用 160k+ 样本进行监督微调（SFT）的模型性能，显著提高了数据效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）通常需要针对特定领域进行适应性调整，而仅依赖监督微调（SFT）的方法成本高昂。本研究旨在探索一种更数据高效的领域自适应方法，以降低成本并提高 LLM 在特定领域的表现。

Method: 本研究应用条件偏好优化（CPO）来模拟一个后编辑工作流，以实现数据高效的领域自适应。具体而言，该方法通过将基础模型的原始输出作为“拒绝”的翻译，将人类批准的翻译记忆库（TM）条目作为“选择”的翻译，来合成偏好对。这种合成的偏好对为模型提供了直接反馈，引导其向领域特定的标准看齐。研究在英-巴西葡语和英-韩语翻译任务上进行了实验。

Result: 实验结果表明，使用 CPO 模拟后编辑工作流的方法在数据效率方面表现出色。仅使用 14.7k 个合成的偏好对，模型在英-巴西葡语和英-韩语翻译任务上取得了与使用 160k+ 样本进行 SFT 的模型相近的性能。这证明了该方法在减少所需数据量方面具有显著优势。

Conclusion: 本研究成功展示了 CPO 在数据高效领域自适应方面的潜力，特别是在机器翻译任务中。通过将 CPO 应用于模拟后编辑工作流，研究人员能够使用远少于传统 SFT 方法的数据量，获得与之相当的性能。尽管研究重点是机器翻译，但该方法具有更广泛的应用前景，可推广到其他需要将模型初始草稿与黄金参考进行对比以进行反馈的生成式任务。

Abstract: LLMs often require adaptation to domain-specific requirements, a process that
can be expensive when relying solely on SFT. We present an empirical study on
applying CPO to simulate a post-editing workflow for data-efficient domain
adaptation. Our approach synthesizes preference pairs by treating the base
model's own raw output as the 'rejected' translation and the human-approved TM
entry as the 'chosen' one. This method provides direct feedback on the model's
current knowledge, guiding it to align with domain-specific standards.
Experiments in English-Brazilian Portuguese and English-Korean show that, by
using just 14.7k preference pairs, the model achieves performance close to that
of a model trained on 160k+ samples with SFT, demonstrating significant data
efficiency. Although we showcase its effectiveness in MT, this application of
CPO naturally generalizes to other generative tasks where a model's initial
drafts can serve as a contrastive signal against a golden reference.

</details>


### [38] [MARAG-R1: Beyond Single Retriever via Reinforcement-Learned Multi-Tool Agentic Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27569)
*Qi Luo,Xiaonan Li,Yuxin Wang,Tingshuo Fan,Yuan Li,Xinchi Chen,Xipeng Qiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）虽然在推理和生成方面表现出色，但受限于静态的预训练数据，存在事实不准确和适应新信息能力较弱的问题。检索增强生成（RAG）通过整合外部知识来解决此问题，但其有效性很大程度上取决于模型访问相关信息的能力。现有RAG系统依赖单一的、具有固定top-k选择的检索器，导致信息获取范围受限且静态。这成为了全面获取外部信息的瓶颈，尤其是在需要语料库级别推理的任务中。为了克服这一限制，我们提出了MARAG-R1，一个基于强化学习的多工具RAG框架，使LLMs能够动态协调多个检索机制，实现更广泛、更精确的信息访问。MARAG-R1配备了四种检索工具——语义搜索、关键词搜索、过滤和聚合——并通过两阶段训练过程（监督微调后进行强化学习）学习如何以及何时使用它们。这种设计使得模型能够交织推理和检索，逐步收集足够的证据进行语料库级别的综合。在GlobalQA、HotpotQA和2WikiMultiHopQA上的实验表明，MARAG-R1在语料库级别推理任务上显著优于强大的基线模型，并取得了新的最先进成果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）虽然在推理和生成方面能力强大，但其固有的静态预训练数据限制了它们获取最新信息和保持事实准确性的能力。检索增强生成（RAG）技术旨在通过结合外部知识来缓解这一问题。然而，现有RAG系统的核心瓶颈在于其单一检索器的局限性，它通常采用固定的top-k选择策略，无法充分挖掘整个语料库的丰富信息，尤其是在需要进行复杂、深层次的语料库级别推理的任务中，这种限制尤为明显。因此，研究如何提升RAG系统在信息获取方面的全面性和精确性，是推动LLMs在需要广泛知识支持的应用中发展的关键。

Method: 为了解决现有RAG系统单一检索器的局限性，我们提出了一种名为MARAG-R1的强化学习多工具RAG框架。该框架的核心在于赋予LLM动态协调多个检索工具的能力，以实现更广泛、更精确的信息获取。MARAG-R1集成了四种不同的检索工具：语义搜索、关键词搜索、过滤和聚合。通过一个两阶段的训练过程，模型学会了如何以及何时有效地运用这些工具。第一阶段是监督微调，用于初步学习检索策略；第二阶段是强化学习，进一步优化模型在复杂推理任务中选择和组合检索工具的能力。这种设计使得模型能够将推理过程与信息检索过程有机地结合起来，通过逐步、迭代地收集和整合信息，最终形成对整个语料库的深入理解和综合分析。

Result: 在GlobalQA、HotpotQA和2WikiMultiHopQA这三个语料库级别推理任务上的实验结果表明，MARAG-R1取得了显著的性能提升。与现有的强大基线模型相比，MARAG-R1在各项评估指标上均表现出优越性，并在这些具有挑战性的任务上刷新了最先进（state-of-the-art）的记录。这证明了MARAG-R1通过多工具协同检索和动态策略学习，能够更有效地获取和利用外部知识，从而极大地增强了LLM在复杂推理场景下的表现。

Conclusion: MARAG-R1通过引入一个基于强化学习的多工具RAG框架，成功解决了现有RAG系统在信息获取方面的局限性，特别是在需要语料库级别推理的任务中。该框架通过动态协调语义搜索、关键词搜索、过滤和聚合等多种检索工具，显著提升了LLM获取和利用外部知识的能力，并在多个基准数据集上取得了最先进的成果。尽管MARAG-R1展现了强大的潜力，但未来仍可进一步探索更复杂的工具组合、更优化的训练策略以及在更多样化的下游任务中的应用。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) excel at reasoning and generation but are
inherently limited by static pretraining data, resulting in factual
inaccuracies and weak adaptability to new information. Retrieval-Augmented
Generation (RAG) addresses this issue by grounding LLMs in external knowledge;
However, the effectiveness of RAG critically depends on whether the model can
adequately access relevant information. Existing RAG systems rely on a single
retriever with fixed top-k selection, restricting access to a narrow and static
subset of the corpus. As a result, this single-retriever paradigm has become
the primary bottleneck for comprehensive external information acquisition,
especially in tasks requiring corpus-level reasoning. To overcome this
limitation, we propose MARAG-R1, a reinforcement-learned multi-tool RAG
framework that enables LLMs to dynamically coordinate multiple retrieval
mechanisms for broader and more precise information access. MARAG-R1 equips the
model with four retrieval tools -- semantic search, keyword search, filtering,
and aggregation -- and learns both how and when to use them through a two-stage
training process: supervised fine-tuning followed by reinforcement learning.
This design allows the model to interleave reasoning and retrieval,
progressively gathering sufficient evidence for corpus-level synthesis.
Experiments on GlobalQA, HotpotQA, and 2WikiMultiHopQA demonstrate that
MARAG-R1 substantially outperforms strong baselines and achieves new
state-of-the-art results in corpus-level reasoning tasks.

</details>


### [39] [SpecAttn: Speculating Sparse Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27641)
*Harsh Shah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SpecAttn是一种创新的、无需训练的方法，通过利用草稿模型在推断过程中计算的注意力权重，识别目标模型中的重要标记，从而实现高效的稀疏注意力。它与现有的投机解码技术无缝集成，通过KL散度层对齐、GPU优化的无排序Top-p标记选择算法以及由预测指导的动态键值缓存修剪，显著减少了计算量。在PG-19数据集上，SpecAttn实现了超过75%的键值缓存访问量减少，同时困惑度仅增加了15.29%，显著优于现有的稀疏注意力方法，证明了投机执行可以有效地提供近似验证，而不会导致显著的性能下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在推理过程中面临着显著的计算瓶颈，这主要是由于自注意力机制的二次复杂性，尤其是在上下文长度不断增加的情况下。这种计算效率低下限制了LLMs在处理长文本和复杂任务时的应用和扩展。因此，有必要开发一种能够有效降低LLM推理成本，同时保持模型性能的新方法。

Method: SpecAttn采用一种无需训练的、与现有投机解码技术相结合的方法来实现高效稀疏注意力。其核心思想是利用草稿模型在投机解码过程中已经计算出的注意力权重来识别对目标模型重要的标记，从而避免不必要的计算。具体来说，SpecAttn包含三个关键技术：1. **KL散度层对齐：** 确保草稿模型和目标模型在不同层之间的注意力分布具有相似性。2. **GPU优化的无排序Top-p标记选择算法：** 基于草稿模型的注意力模式，高效地选择最重要的标记，无需进行排序操作。3. **动态键值缓存修剪：** 根据上述识别出的重要标记，动态地修剪键值缓存，进一步减少内存占用和计算量。整个过程与标准的投机解码流水线集成，无需额外的训练。

Result: 在PG-19数据集上的实验结果表明，SpecAttn取得了显著的性能提升。与基线方法相比，SpecAttn实现了超过75%的键值缓存访问量减少，同时困惑度（perplexity）仅增加了15.29%。这一结果表明，SpecAttn在大幅降低计算成本的同时，能够有效地保持模型的输出质量，优于现有的稀疏注意力方法。

Conclusion: SpecAttn的实验结果证明，通过利用投机解码过程中已有的计算工作，可以有效地实现稀疏注意力，而无需额外的训练。该方法在显著降低键值缓存访问量方面表现出色，同时保持了可接受的模型性能。这表明投机执行可以被增强，以在不显著降低性能的情况下提供近似验证，为提高大型语言模型的推理效率提供了有前景的方向。未来的工作可以探索将SpecAttn应用于更广泛的模型架构和任务，并进一步优化其效率。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) face significant computational bottlenecks
during inference due to the quadratic complexity of self-attention mechanisms,
particularly as context lengths increase. We introduce SpecAttn, a novel
training-free approach that seamlessly integrates with existing speculative
decoding techniques to enable efficient sparse attention in pre-trained
transformers. Our key insight is to exploit the attention weights already
computed by the draft model during speculative decoding to identify important
tokens for the target model, eliminating redundant computation while
maintaining output quality. SpecAttn employs three core techniques: KL
divergence-based layer alignment between draft and target models, a
GPU-optimized sorting-free algorithm for top-p token selection from draft
attention patterns, and dynamic key-value cache pruning guided by these
predictions. By leveraging the computational work already performed in standard
speculative decoding pipelines, SpecAttn achieves over 75% reduction in
key-value cache accesses with a mere 15.29% increase in perplexity on the PG-19
dataset, significantly outperforming existing sparse attention methods. Our
approach demonstrates that speculative execution can be enhanced to provide
approximate verification without significant performance degradation.

</details>


### [40] [Continuous Autoregressive Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27688)
*Chenze Shao,Darren Li,Fandong Meng,Jie Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLM的效率受限于其逐个token的生成过程。本文提出连续自回归语言模型（CALM），将离散的下一个token预测转变为连续的下一个向量预测。CALM通过高保真自编码器将K个token压缩成一个连续向量，从而将生成步数减少K倍。该模型在性能-计算权衡方面有显著提升，并在更低的计算成本下实现了与强离散基线相当的性能，为构建超高效语言模型提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型（LLMs）的效率受到其顺序生成过程的根本性限制。为了克服这一瓶颈，需要一种新的LLM扩展设计思路，即提升每个生成步骤的语义带宽。

Method: CALM模型将离散的下一个token预测转变为连续的下一个向量预测。具体而言，它使用一个高保真自编码器将K个连续的token压缩成一个单一的连续向量，并能够以超过99.9%的准确率重建原始token。这使得模型能够将语言建模为连续向量序列而非离散token序列，从而将生成步数减少K倍。CALM还开发了一个全面的无似然框架，以支持在连续域中的鲁棒训练、评估和可控采样。

Result: 实验表明，CALM显著改善了性能-计算权衡。在显著降低计算成本的同时，CALM达到了强离散基线模型的性能水平。

Conclusion: CALM的实验结果证明了下一个向量预测作为实现超高效语言模型的一种强大且可扩展的途径。这一范式转变有望在不牺牲性能的情况下大幅提高语言模型的效率。

Abstract: The efficiency of large language models (LLMs) is fundamentally limited by
their sequential, token-by-token generation process. We argue that overcoming
this bottleneck requires a new design axis for LLM scaling: increasing the
semantic bandwidth of each generative step. To this end, we introduce
Continuous Autoregressive Language Models (CALM), a paradigm shift from
discrete next-token prediction to continuous next-vector prediction. CALM uses
a high-fidelity autoencoder to compress a chunk of K tokens into a single
continuous vector, from which the original tokens can be reconstructed with
over 99.9\% accuracy. This allows us to model language as a sequence of
continuous vectors instead of discrete tokens, which reduces the number of
generative steps by a factor of K. The paradigm shift necessitates a new
modeling toolkit; therefore, we develop a comprehensive likelihood-free
framework that enables robust training, evaluation, and controllable sampling
in the continuous domain. Experiments show that CALM significantly improves the
performance-compute trade-off, achieving the performance of strong discrete
baselines at a significantly lower computational cost. More importantly, these
findings establish next-vector prediction as a powerful and scalable pathway
towards ultra-efficient language models. Code:
https://github.com/shaochenze/calm. Project:
https://shaochenze.github.io/blog/2025/CALM.

</details>


### [41] [LIBMoE: A Library for comprehensive benchmarking Mixture of Experts in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2411.00918)
*Nam V. Nguyen,Thong T. Doan,Luong Tran,Van Nguyen,Quang Pham*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Mixture of Experts (MoE) 架构在扩展大型语言模型方面至关重要，但训练和评估成本高昂，限制了研究。本文提出了 LibMoE，一个统一、高效、可扩展的 MoE 研究框架，支持预训练和稀疏升维。该框架提供了分析路由和专家动态的工具，并进行了全面的分析，包括路由动态、轻量级初始化对负载均衡的影响以及训练机制的差异。LibMoE 降低了 MoE 研究的门槛，标准化了评估，并通过深入分析促进了该领域的进步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出 LibMoE，一个统一的框架，用于可复现、高效和可扩展的 MoE 研究，支持预训练和稀疏升维（sparse-upcycling）两种模式。该框架不仅提供了统一的实现，还提供了透明的分析工具，用于探究路由（routing）和专家（expert）的动态。基于此，研究人员进行了全面的分析，涵盖了三个维度：(i) 路由动态，包括专家选择模式、路由的稳定性和最优性，以及路由熵如何揭示任务专业化和专家多样性；(ii) 轻量级初始化对负载均衡的影响，展示了路由器初始化方式的细微变化如何影响早期专家利用率；(iii) 训练机制的差异，揭示了稀疏升维和完全预训练在路由模式和稳定性方面存在的差异。

Result: 通过 LibMoE 框架，研究人员进行了全面的分析，主要发现了以下几点：(i) 在路由动态方面，揭示了专家选择模式、路由稳定性和最优性，并证明了路由熵与任务专业化和专家多样性之间的关系；(ii) 证明了轻量级初始化策略对早期专家利用率和负载均衡有显著影响；(iii) 比较了稀疏升维和完全预训练两种训练机制，发现它们在路由模式和稳定性方面表现出不同的特性。这些分析结果为理解和优化 MoE 架构提供了宝贵的见解。

Conclusion: LibMoE 框架通过降低 MoE 研究的准入门槛、标准化评估流程，并结合全面的分析，极大地促进了 MoE 领域的研究。它为未来的创新提供了可靠的基准，并使更广泛的研究社区能够参与到 MoE 的前沿研究中。

Abstract: Mixture of experts (MoE) architectures have become a cornerstone for scaling
up and are a key component in most large language models such as GPT-OSS,
DeepSeek-V3, Llama-4, and Gemini-2.5. However, systematic research on MoE
remains severely constrained by the prohibitive computational costs of training
and evaluation, restricting large-scale studies accessible to most researchers.
We introduce LibMoE, a unified framework for reproducible, efficient, and
extensible MoE research that supports both pretraining and sparse-upcycling
regimes. Beyond unified implementations, the framework provides transparent
analytical tools for probing routing and expert dynamics. Leveraging this
foundation, we conduct a comprehensive analysis along three dimensions: (i)
routing dynamics, covering expert selection patterns, routing stability and
optimality, and how routing entropy reveals task specialization and expert
diversity; (ii) the effect of lightweight initialization on load balancing,
demonstrating how subtle changes in router initialization shape early expert
utilization; and (iii) training regime differences, revealing how sparse
upcycling and full pretraining exhibit distinct routing patterns and stability
profiles. By lowering the barrier to entry and standardizing evaluation, along
with our comprehensive analysis, LibMoE broadens access to MoE research and
establishes a reliable benchmark to guide future innovations. Project page:
https://fsoft-aic.github.io/fsoft-LibMoE.github.io.

### [42] [Scalable Best-of-N Selection for Large Language Models via Self-Certainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2502.18581)
*Zhewei Kang,Xuandong Zhao,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“自确信”（self-certainty）的新型高效指标，用于在无需外部奖励模型的情况下评估大型语言模型（LLM）生成响应的质量。该方法利用LLM输出的固有概率分布来衡量其生成置信度，并通过实验证明，在增加样本量N的情况下，自确信指标能够有效扩展，并且优于传统的奖励模型，同时还能提升链式思考（chain-of-thought）的表现，并能应用于传统自洽性（self-consistency）方法难以处理的开放式生成任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的大型语言模型（LLM）在推理任务中，通常采用“N选最佳”（Best-of-N）技术来提升性能，但这需要增加测试时间的计算量。现有的最佳方法依赖计算成本高昂的奖励模型来评估和选择响应。而一些无需奖励模型的替代方法，如自洽性（self-consistency）和通用自洽性（universal self-consistency），在处理开放式生成任务或有效扩展方面存在局限性。因此，研究旨在解决这些限制，寻找一种更高效、可扩展且适用于开放式任务的LLM响应评估和选择方法。

Method: 研究提出了“自确信”（self-certainty）这一新指标，它不依赖外部奖励模型，而是利用LLM输出的固有概率分布来估计响应的质量。其核心假设是，跨多个样本聚合的更高的分布自确信度与更高的响应准确性相关，因为它反映了模型对其生成输出的更大信心。通过在各种推理任务上进行广泛的实验来验证该方法的有效性。实验设置包括与链式思考（chain-of-thought）的结合，以及在不同样本量N下的性能评估，并与现有的奖励模型方法和自洽性方法进行比较。

Result: 实验结果表明，“自确信”指标具有以下优点：1. 能够有效地随着样本量N的增加而扩展，其扩展方式类似于奖励模型，但没有计算开销。2. 能够与链式思考（chain-of-thought）相结合，在贪婪解码的基础上进一步提升推理性能。3. 能够泛化到传统自洽性方法表现不佳的开放式生成任务。研究通过大量实验证明了自确信在提高LLM推理能力方面的有效性和实用性。

Conclusion: 研究成功开发并验证了一种名为“自确信”的新型LLM推理增强方法。该方法通过利用LLM输出的概率分布来衡量生成响应的置信度，无需昂贵的奖励模型，有效解决了现有方法的计算开销和在开放式任务上的局限性。实验结果表明，“自确信”在扩展性、与链式思考的结合以及处理开放式任务方面均表现出色，为提高LLM的推理能力提供了一种实用且高效的解决方案。未来的工作可以进一步探索自确信在更多类型的LLM任务和模型上的应用潜力。

Abstract: Best-of-N selection is a key technique for improving the reasoning
performance of Large Language Models (LLMs) through increased test-time
computation. Current state-of-the-art methods often employ computationally
intensive reward models for response evaluation and selection. Reward-free
alternatives, like self-consistency and universal self-consistency, are limited
in their ability to handle open-ended generation tasks or scale effectively. To
address these limitations, we propose self-certainty, a novel and efficient
metric that leverages the inherent probability distribution of LLM outputs to
estimate response quality without requiring external reward models. We
hypothesize that higher distributional self-certainty, aggregated across
multiple samples, correlates with improved response accuracy, as it reflects
greater confidence in the generated output. Through extensive experiments on
various reasoning tasks, we demonstrate that self-certainty (1) scales
effectively with increasing sample size N, akin to reward models but without
the computational overhead; (2) complements chain-of-thought, improving
reasoning performance beyond greedy decoding; and (3) generalizes to open-ended
tasks where traditional self-consistency methods fall short. Our findings
establish self-certainty as a practical and efficient way for improving LLM
reasoning capabilities. The code is available at
https://github.com/backprop07/Self-Certainty

### [43] [(How) Do Language Models Track State?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2503.02854)
*Belinda Z. Li,Zifan Carl Guo,Jacob Andreas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Transformer LMs can learn to track evolving states, a capability crucial for tasks like storytelling and code generation. This paper investigates how LMs achieve this by studying permutation composition, a problem reducible to many other state-tracking tasks. The study reveals that LMs consistently adopt one of two main strategies: an "associative scan" mechanism similar to theoretical models, or a hybrid approach that uses permutation parity to prune outputs before applying an associative scan. The research demonstrates that LMs trained with the pure associative scan generalize better and converge faster. Furthermore, the paper shows that these mechanisms can be predicted and controlled through targeted intermediate training tasks, suggesting that Transformer LMs can learn efficient and interpretable state-tracking methods.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The research addresses the question of how Transformer language models (LMs) acquire the ability to track unobserved states in evolving systems, a capability that appears necessary for complex tasks like storytelling and code generation. Understanding this state-tracking mechanism is crucial for comprehending and improving the internal workings of LMs, especially given their potential for diverse applications. The paper focuses on permutation composition as a model problem, as it is algebraically simple yet general enough to encompass various state-tracking challenges, including finite automata simulation and boolean expression evaluation.

Method: The study analyzes LMs trained or fine-tuned on the task of permutation composition. Permutation composition involves determining the final order of a set of objects after a series of swaps. The researchers observed the internal mechanisms employed by these LMs to solve this task. They identified two primary state-tracking strategies that emerge: one closely mirroring the "associative scan" construction proposed in prior theoretical work (Liu et al., 2023; Merrill et al., 2024), and another that initially utilizes permutation parity to reduce the output space, followed by an associative scan for refinement. The study also explored methods to influence which strategy an LM adopts by using intermediate training tasks designed to either encourage or discourage the use of parity heuristics.

Result: The experiments showed that LMs trained using the pure associative scan mechanism tend to exhibit superior generalization capabilities and faster convergence rates compared to those using the hybrid parity-and-scan approach. The study successfully demonstrated that by employing specific intermediate training tasks, it is possible to steer the LMs towards adopting either the associative scan or the parity-enhanced scan strategy. This indicates a level of predictability and controllability over the learned state-tracking mechanisms.

Conclusion: This research concludes that Transformer LMs are capable of learning efficient and interpretable state-tracking mechanisms, exemplified by their performance on permutation composition. The study not only identifies two distinct learned algorithms for state tracking but also provides evidence that the emergence of these mechanisms can be anticipated and guided. The findings suggest that by understanding and manipulating the training process, we can potentially enhance the state-tracking abilities of LMs, leading to improved performance on complex tasks that require maintaining and updating an internal world model.

Abstract: Transformer language models (LMs) exhibit behaviors -- from storytelling to
code generation -- that seem to require tracking the unobserved state of an
evolving world. How do they do this? We study state tracking in LMs trained or
fine-tuned to compose permutations (i.e., to compute the order of a set of
objects after a sequence of swaps). Despite the simple algebraic structure of
this problem, many other tasks (e.g., simulation of finite automata and
evaluation of boolean expressions) can be reduced to permutation composition,
making it a natural model for state tracking in general. We show that LMs
consistently learn one of two state tracking mechanisms for this task. The
first closely resembles the "associative scan" construction used in recent
theoretical work by Liu et al. (2023) and Merrill et al. (2024). The second
uses an easy-to-compute feature (permutation parity) to partially prune the
space of outputs, and then refines this with an associative scan. LMs that
learn the former algorithm tend to generalize better and converge faster, and
we show how to steer LMs toward one or the other with intermediate training
tasks that encourage or suppress the heuristics. Our results demonstrate that
transformer LMs, whether pre-trained or fine-tuned, can learn to implement
efficient and interpretable state-tracking mechanisms, and the emergence of
these mechanisms can be predicted and controlled.

</details>


### [44] [FUSE : A Ridge and Random Forest-Based Metric for Evaluating MT in Indigenous Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.00021)
*Rahul Raja,Arpita Vats*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RaaVa团队在AmericasNLP 2025机器翻译（MT）评估共享任务中，凭借其提出的融合了岭回归和梯度提升的特征并集评分器（FUSE）获得了第一名。FUSE通过整合词汇、语音、语义和模糊标记相似性特征，并结合学习范式，能够更好地评估进入美洲原住民语言的机器翻译质量，尤其是在处理多式性、复杂形态和非标准化拼写等独特挑战方面，其表现优于BLEU、TER和ChrF等传统指标，与人类评估的相关性更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的自动机器翻译（MT）评估指标（如BLEU、TER和ChrF）在处理进入美洲原住民语言的翻译时效果不佳。这些语言通常具有多式性、复杂的形态结构和非标准化的拼写，导致传统指标难以捕捉翻译的深层语义和流畅性。因此，迫切需要开发一种更有效的评估方法，能够更好地与人类判断保持一致，尤其是在低资源环境下。

Method: 该研究提出了特征并集评分器（FUSE）框架，该框架整合了岭回归和梯度提升两种机器学习模型来评估翻译质量。FUSE的创新之处在于结合了多种语言相似性特征，包括词汇、语音、语义和模糊标记相似性。此外，还探索了五种利用不同语言特征和学习范式组合的替代方法。实验中，在人类标注的开发数据集上训练监督模型，并在独立的测试数据集上进行评估。FUSE框架还纳入了多语言句子嵌入和语音编码，以期更好地与人类评估保持一致。

Result: FUSE框架在AmericasNLP 2025评估任务中表现出色，在与人类标注者的相关性方面（皮尔逊相关系数）取得了总体第一名的成绩。结果表明，FUSE在皮尔逊和斯皮尔曼相关系数上均 consistently 优于其他方法，与人类判断保持了更高的一致性。这证明了FUSE作为一种基于语言学特征且具有鲁棒性的评估解决方案，在低资源场景下进行机器翻译评估的有效性。

Conclusion: FUSE框架通过融合多种语言特征和先进的机器学习模型（岭回归和梯度提升），成功解决了进入美洲原住民语言的机器翻译评估难题，并在AmericasNLP 2025竞赛中取得了显著成果。该方法在与人类判断的相关性方面表现优越，为低资源、语言特征独特的语言翻译评估提供了更可靠、更符合语言学原理的解决方案。未来的工作可以进一步探索更多样的语言特征和模型，以期进一步提升评估的准确性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: This paper presents the winning submission of the RaaVa team to the
AmericasNLP 2025 Shared Task 3 on Automatic Evaluation Metrics for Machine
Translation (MT) into Indigenous Languages of America, where our system ranked
first overall based on average Pearson correlation with the human annotations.
We introduce Feature-Union Scorer (FUSE) for Evaluation, FUSE integrates Ridge
regression and Gradient Boosting to model translation quality. In addition to
FUSE, we explore five alternative approaches leveraging different combinations
of linguistic similarity features and learning paradigms. FUSE Score highlights
the effectiveness of combining lexical, phonetic, semantic, and fuzzy token
similarity with learning-based modeling to improve MT evaluation for
morphologically rich and low-resource languages. MT into Indigenous languages
poses unique challenges due to polysynthesis, complex morphology, and
non-standardized orthography. Conventional automatic metrics such as BLEU, TER,
and ChrF often fail to capture deeper aspects like semantic adequacy and
fluency. Our proposed framework, formerly referred to as FUSE, incorporates
multilingual sentence embeddings and phonological encodings to better align
with human evaluation. We train supervised models on human-annotated
development sets and evaluate held-out test data. Results show that FUSE
consistently achieves higher Pearson and Spearman correlations with human
judgments, offering a robust and linguistically informed solution for MT
evaluation in low-resource settings.

</details>


### [45] [HELIOS: Adaptive Model And Early-Exit Selection for Efficient LLM Inference Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.10724)
*Avinash Kumar,Shashank Nag,Jason Clemons,Lizy John,Poulami Das*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EE-LLMs通过允许token在中间层提前退出以提高推理吞吐量，但计算和内存节省有限。现有的EE-LLM框架使用单一模型，并且需要加载所有层权重，限制了批处理大小。HELIOS框架通过利用多个模型和贪婪地允许低置信度token提前退出，提高了EE-LLMs的吞吐量和批处理大小。HELIOS通过实时分析和自适应模型切换，实现了1.48倍的吞吐量提升和15.14倍的批处理大小增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EE-LLM框架在提高推理吞吐量方面存在计算和内存节省有限的问题。单一模型在处理不提前退出的token时存在延迟瓶颈，并且需要加载所有层权重，这限制了批处理大小的扩展。

Method: HELIOS框架提出了一种新的方法来提高EE-LLM的吞吐量和批处理大小。它利用了两个关键的见解：1. 多个模型之间的提前退出具有互补性，HELIOS使用多个模型并动态切换以最大化提前退出的token数量并最小化延迟。2. 即使token置信度不高，其预测结果在经过更多层后也可能保持不变，HELIOS允许这类token提前退出，并只加载最有可能使用的层权重，从而节省内存并增加批处理大小。HELIOS还使用实时分析来准确识别提前退出分布，并实时跟踪token以自适应地切换模型。

Result: 与现有的EE-LLM框架相比，HELIOS实现了1.48倍的吞吐量提升和15.14倍的批处理大小增加。

Conclusion: HELIOS框架通过多模型协作和贪婪的提前退出策略，显著提高了EE-LLM的性能，解决了现有方法的局限性。该框架通过提高吞吐量和扩展批处理大小，为实现高吞吐量EE-LLM提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Early-Exit Large Language Models (EE-LLMs) enable high throughput inference
by allowing tokens to exit early at intermediate layers. However, their
throughput is limited by the computational and memory savings. Existing EE-LLM
frameworks rely on a single model and therefore, their token generation
latencies are bottlenecked by tokens that do not exit early and traverse
additional layers. Moreover, early exits are only known at runtime and depend
on the request. Therefore, these frameworks load the weights of all model
layers even though large portions remain unused when tokens exit early. The
lack of memory savings limit us from scaling the batch sizes.
  We propose $\textit{HELIOS}$, a framework that improves both token generation
latency and batch sizes to enable high-throughput in EE-LLMs. HELIOS exploits
two insights. $\textit{First}$, early exits are often complimentary across
models, tokens that do not exit early on one model often take an early-exit on
another. HELIOS employs multiple models and dynamically switches between them
to collectively maximize the number of tokens that exit early, and minimize
token generation latencies. $\textit{Second}$, even when a predicted token does
not exit early due to poor confidence, it often remains unchanged even after
additional layer traversal. HELIOS greedily allows such tokens to exit early
and only loads the weights of the most likely to be used layers, yielding
memory savings which is then re-purposed to increase batch sizes. HELIOS
employs real-time profiling to accurately identify the early-exit
distributions, and adaptively switches between models by tracking tokens in
real-time to minimize the performance degradation caused by greedy model
loading and exiting. Our evaluations show that HELIOS achieves $1.48\times$
higher throughput and $15.14\times$ larger batch size compared to existing
EE-LLM frameworks.

</details>


### [46] [Cancer-Myth: Evaluating Large Language Models on Patient Questions with False Presuppositions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.11373)
*Wang Bill Zhu,Tianqi Chen,Xinyan Velocity Yu,Ching Ying Lin,Jade Law,Mazen Jizzini,Jorge J. Nieva,Ruishan Liu,Robin Jia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理癌症患者的个性化医疗问题时存在识别和纠正错误前提的能力不足，即使是领先模型也难以超过43%的准确率。虽然提示工程等缓解策略可以提高在包含错误前提的问题上的准确性，但也会导致在正常问题上的误报率增加和整体性能下降，凸显了在医疗AI系统中增强鲁棒性和安全性的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着癌症患者越来越多地使用大型语言模型（LLMs）获取医疗信息，评估LLMs处理复杂、个性化问题的能力变得至关重要。现有医学基准测试未能充分评估LLMs处理包含患者具体信息的真实患者问题的能力，特别是错误前提的识别和纠正方面，这可能对安全的医疗决策构成风险。

Method: 研究人员首先由三名血液肿瘤科医生评估了来自真实患者的癌症相关问题。为了系统地研究LLMs在识别错误前提方面的局限性，他们引入了一个名为Cancer-Myth的专家验证数据集，包含585个带有错误前提的癌症相关问题。接着，为了研究缓解策略，研究人员构建了一个包含150个问题的Cancer-Myth-NFP数据集，以确认其中不存在错误前提。他们测试了包括GPT-5、Gemini-2.5-Pro和Claude-4-Sonnet在内的前沿LLMs。随后，他们评估了包括添加预防性提示和GEPA优化在内的缓解策略，并在Cancer-Myth和Cancer-Myth-NFP数据集上进行了测试，同时也在其他医学基准测试上评估了性能变化。

Result: 在Cancer-Myth数据集上，包括GPT-5、Gemini-2.5-Pro和Claude-4-Sonnet在内的所有前沿LLM纠正错误前提的准确率均不超过43%。在Cancer-Myth-NFP数据集上，虽然采用提示工程等缓解策略可以将Cancer-Myth的准确率提高到80%，但同时会导致Cancer-Myth-NFP数据集中41%的问题被错误识别为包含错误前提，并且在其他医学基准测试上出现10%的相对性能下降。

Conclusion: 研究表明，当前LLMs在处理包含错误前提的癌症患者问题时存在显著的可靠性差距。虽然提示工程等缓解策略可以在一定程度上提高处理错误前提问题的能力，但并非可靠的解决方案，并且可能引入新的问题。这项研究强调了在医疗AI系统中开发更强大的安全措施和更鲁棒的评估基准的迫切需求，以确保患者安全和有效的医疗决策。

Abstract: Cancer patients are increasingly turning to large language models (LLMs) for
medical information, making it critical to assess how well these models handle
complex, personalized questions. However, current medical benchmarks focus on
medical exams or consumer-searched questions and do not evaluate LLMs on real
patient questions with patient details. In this paper, we first have three
hematology-oncology physicians evaluate cancer-related questions drawn from
real patients. While LLM responses are generally accurate, the models
frequently fail to recognize or address false presuppositions in the questions,
posing risks to safe medical decision-making. To study this limitation
systematically, we introduce Cancer-Myth, an expert-verified adversarial
dataset of 585 cancer-related questions with false presuppositions. On this
benchmark, no frontier LLM -- including GPT-5, Gemini-2.5-Pro, and
Claude-4-Sonnet -- corrects these false presuppositions more than $43\%$ of the
time. To study mitigation strategies, we further construct a 150-question
Cancer-Myth-NFP set, in which physicians confirm the absence of false
presuppositions. We find typical mitigation strategies, such as adding
precautionary prompts with GEPA optimization, can raise accuracy on Cancer-Myth
to $80\%$, but at the cost of misidentifying presuppositions in $41\%$ of
Cancer-Myth-NFP questions and causing a $10\%$ relative performance drop on
other medical benchmarks. These findings highlight a critical gap in the
reliability of LLMs, show that prompting alone is not a reliable remedy for
false presuppositions, and underscore the need for more robust safeguards in
medical AI systems.

### [47] [Integrating Video and Text: A Balanced Approach to Multimodal Summary Generation and Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.06594)
*Galann Pennec,Zhengyuan Liu,Nicholas Asher,Philippe Muller,Nancy F. Chen*

TL;DR: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) 在处理复杂的电视节目等多模态输入时，在平衡视觉和文本信息方面存在挑战。本文提出了一种零样本视频到文本摘要方法，通过构建自身的剧本表示来整合关键视频时刻、对话和角色信息。该方法能同时生成剧本并识别角色，仅使用音频、视频和文本作为输入。为解决现有摘要指标评估多模态内容不足的问题，本文引入了多模态指标 MFactSum，并用其评估了剧本摘要在 SummScreen3D 数据集上的表现，结果显示该方法比 Gemini 1.5 等先进 VLM 效果更好，摘要包含的视觉信息多 20%，而输入的视频量减少了 75%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Vision-Language Models (VLMs) 在处理如电视节目这样的复杂多模态输入时，难以有效地平衡视觉和文本信息，导致生成的摘要无法全面捕捉原始内容。特别是在电视节目摘要场景下，需要同时整合关键的视觉片段、对话内容以及角色信息，这对于现有模型来说是一个巨大的挑战。因此，需要一种新的方法来更有效地处理这些复杂的多模态数据，并生成信息丰富且准确的摘要。

Method: 本文提出了一种零样本视频到文本摘要方法。该方法的核心是构建一个电视节目集锦的剧本表示，能够有效地整合关键的视频时刻、对话和角色信息。与以往的方法不同，该模型能够同时生成剧本并识别其中出现的角色，而无需任何预先的标注数据（零样本），仅依赖音频、视频和文本转录。此外，为了更准确地评估多模态摘要的质量，本文还引入了一个新的多模态评估指标 MFactSum，该指标能够同时从视觉和文本两个模态评估摘要的相关性。最后，在 SummScreen3D 数据集上，使用 MFactSum 指标对所提出的剧本摘要方法进行了评估，并与包括 Gemini 1.5 在内的最先进的 VLM 进行了比较。

Result: 在 SummScreen3D 数据集上的实验结果表明，本文提出的基于剧本表示的零样本视频摘要方法优于现有的最先进的 VLM。具体来说，生成的摘要包含了 20% 更多的相关视觉信息，同时输入的视频量减少了 75%。MFactSum 指标的引入也证明了其在评估多模态摘要方面的有效性，突显了该方法在内容相关性和效率方面的优势。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种创新的零样本视频到文本摘要方法，通过构建剧本表示来有效整合多模态信息，并引入了新的多模态评估指标 MFactSum。该方法在电视节目摘要任务上取得了显著的进步，能够生成包含更多相关视觉信息且效率更高的摘要。未来的工作可以探索将此方法应用于其他类型的多模态内容，并进一步提升剧本生成和角色识别的准确性。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) often struggle to balance visual and textual
information when summarizing complex multimodal inputs, such as entire TV show
episodes. In this paper, we propose a zero-shot video-to-text summarization
approach that builds its own screenplay representation of an episode,
effectively integrating key video moments, dialogue, and character information
into a unified document. Unlike previous approaches, we simultaneously generate

and transcripts as input. Additionally, we highlight that existing

To address this, we introduce MFactSum, a multimodal metric that evaluates
summaries with respect to both vision and text modalities. Using MFactSum, we

superiority against state-of-the-art VLMs such as Gemini 1.5 by generating
summaries containing 20% more relevant visual information while requiring 75%

### [48] [VeriFastScore: Speeding up long-form factuality evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.16973)
*Rishanth Rajendhran,Amir Zadeh,Matthew Sarte,Chuan Li,Mohit Iyyer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 现有的事实核查指标（如 FactScore 和 VeriScore）在评估长篇文本的事实准确性时，需要将文本分解为原子声明并逐一核查，这会导致大量的语言模型调用和过长的评估时间（单篇响应超过 100 秒），限制了其在大规模评估和训练场景中的应用。为解决此问题，研究者提出了 VeriFastScore，该方法利用合成数据微调 Llama3.1 8B 模型，使其能够同时从文本中提取和核查所有可验证的声明，并利用 Google 搜索作为证据。研究发现，由于任务的复杂性（模型需要处理约 4000 个 token 的证据，并同时完成声明分解、可验证性判断和事实核查），该任务无法通过少样本提示（few-shot prompting）的闭源语言模型来解决。然而，微调后的 VeriFastScore 模型在示例层面（r=0.80）和系统层面（r=0.94）均与原始 VeriScore 流程表现出高度相关性，同时评估速度提升了 6.6 倍（不包括证据检索则为 9.9 倍）。为了推动未来的事实核查研究，研究者公开了 VeriFastScore 模型和合成数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长篇文本事实核查指标，如 FactScore 和 VeriScore，虽然能够提供可解释的评估，但其工作流程涉及将输入响应分解为原子声明，并对每个声明进行单独验证。这种方法会导致大量的语言模型调用，并显著增加评估时间，单篇响应的评估时间可能超过 100 秒。这种效率低下和耗时的问题严重限制了这些指标在大规模评估和训练场景中的实际应用，使得研究者难以快速迭代和改进模型。因此，研究的动机在于开发一种更快速、更具可扩展性的事实核查方法，以满足实际应用的需求。

Method: 该研究提出了 VeriFastScore，一种旨在提高长篇文本事实核查效率的新方法。VeriFastScore 的核心在于利用合成数据对 Llama3.1 8B 模型进行微调。具体而言，该方法首先利用 Google 搜索获取与输入文本相关的证据。然后，微调后的模型能够同时执行两个关键任务：1. **声明提取**：从给定的文本中识别出所有可被验证的事实声明。2. **声明核查**：将提取出的声明与从 Google 搜索获取的证据进行比对，判断其真实性。研究者特别指出，由于该任务的复杂性——模型需要处理平均约 4000 个 token 的证据，并且需要同时完成声明的分解、可验证性判断以及与证据的核对——仅通过少样本提示（few-shot prompting）的方式，使用闭源语言模型是无法有效解决的。因此，通过微调的方式来训练模型具备这种综合能力是必要的。最后，研究者公开了 VeriFastScore 模型和用于训练的合成数据集，以支持未来的相关研究。

Result: 研究结果表明，VeriFastScore 在评估长篇文本的事实准确性方面取得了显著成效。与原始的 VeriScore 评估流程相比，VeriFastScore 在示例层面（单个响应的评估）与 VeriScore 的相关性达到了 r=0.80，在系统层面（整体评估结果）的相关性更是高达 r=0.94。这意味着 VeriFastScore 能够高度一致地反映 VeriScore 的评估结果。更重要的是，VeriFastScore 在效率上取得了巨大提升，其整体评估速度比 VeriScore 快了 6.6 倍。如果排除证据检索的时间，模型本身的推理速度则比 VeriScore 快了 9.9 倍。这些结果证明了 VeriFastScore 在保持高准确性的同时，显著提高了评估的速度和可扩展性。

Conclusion: VeriFastScore 的提出和实现标志着长篇文本事实核查领域的一项重要进展。该方法通过利用合成数据微调 Llama3.1 8B 模型，成功解决了现有方法在效率和可扩展性方面的瓶颈，实现了在保持高评估准确性的同时，大幅提升了评估速度。研究证明，通过微调，模型能够有效处理复杂的核查任务，包括从大量证据中提取和验证声明，这是少样本提示无法达到的。VeriFastScore 在与 VeriScore 的高度相关性（r=0.80 示例层面，r=0.94 系统层面）和显著的速度提升（6.6x 整体，9.9x 排除检索）上得到了体现。研究者公开模型和数据集的行为，也为社区提供了宝贵的资源，有助于推动未来事实核查技术的研究与发展。尽管如此，研究中可能存在的局限性（例如，对 Google 搜索结果的依赖性、合成数据的代表性等）以及未来可以进一步探索的方向（如提升模型在处理歧义和隐含信息时的鲁棒性、进一步优化证据检索和利用的效率等）仍值得关注。

Abstract: Metrics like FactScore and VeriScore that evaluate long-form factuality
operate by decomposing an input response into atomic claims and then
individually verifying each claim. While effective and interpretable, these
methods incur numerous LLM calls and can take upwards of 100 seconds to
evaluate a single response, limiting their practicality in large-scale
evaluation and training scenarios. To address this, we propose VeriFastScore,
which leverages synthetic data to fine-tune Llama3.1 8B for simultaneously
extracting and verifying all verifiable claims within a given text based on
evidence from Google Search. We show that this task cannot be solved via
few-shot prompting with closed LLMs due to its complexity: the model receives
~4K tokens of evidence on average and needs to concurrently decompose claims,
judge their verifiability, and verify them against noisy evidence. However, our
fine-tuned VeriFastScore model demonstrates strong correlation with the
original VeriScore pipeline at both the example level (r=0.80) and system level
(r=0.94) while achieving an overall speedup of 6.6x (9.9x excluding evidence
retrieval) over VeriScore. To facilitate future factuality research, we
publicly release our VeriFastScore model and synthetic datasets.

</details>


### [49] [Token Distillation: Attention-aware Input Embeddings For New Tokens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.20133)
*Konstantin Dobler,Desmond Elliott,Gerard de Melo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 当前语言模型使用静态词汇表，在处理领域外的数据时表现不佳且计算成本高。现有方法通过添加新词元来解决此问题，但需要昂贵的进一步训练。我们提出了Token Distillation，通过蒸馏原始分词表示来快速学习高质量的新词元嵌入，实验证明该方法优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型依赖于预训练时确定的静态词汇表，这会导致在原始词汇表中代表性不足的领域（如专业领域、新兴语言等）的性能下降和计算成本增加。虽然可以通过添加新词元来解决此问题，但现有的嵌入初始化方法需要昂贵的进一步训练或额外模块的预训练，这使得新词元的引入成本很高。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为Token Distillation的方法。该方法通过蒸馏（distilling）原始分词（tokenization）得到的表示，来快速学习新词元的高质量输入嵌入。这种方法避免了对额外模块进行昂贵的预训练或进一步训练。

Result: 在对一系列开放权重模型进行的广泛实验中，Token Distillation方法被证明优于包括强基线在内的现有方法。具体实验结果表明，该方法能够有效地为新词元学习到高质量的嵌入，从而提升模型在特定领域上的表现。

Conclusion: Token Distillation是一种有效且高效的方法，能够为现有语言模型快速学习高质量的新词元嵌入，解决了静态词汇表带来的性能和成本问题。该方法在多种开放权重模型上的实验表现优于现有技术，展示了其广泛的应用前景和潜力。未来的工作可以进一步探索该方法在不同类型模型和任务上的应用，以及进一步优化蒸馏过程以获得更好的性能。

Abstract: Current language models rely on static vocabularies determined at pretraining
time, which can lead to decreased performance and increased computational cost
for domains underrepresented in the original vocabulary. New tokens can be
added to solve this problem, when coupled with a good initialization for their
new embeddings. However, existing embedding initialization methods require
expensive further training or pretraining of additional modules. In this paper,
we propose Token Distillation and show that by distilling representations
obtained using the original tokenization, we can quickly learn high-quality
input embeddings for new tokens. Experimental results with a wide range of
open-weight models show that Token Distillation outperforms even strong
baselines.

### [50] [AstroVisBench: A Code Benchmark for Scientific Computing and Visualization in Astronomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.20538)
*Sebastian Antony Joseph,Syed Murtaza Husain,Stella S. R. Offner,Stéphanie Juneau,Paul Torrey,Adam S. Bolton,Juan P. Farias,Niall Gaffney,Greg Durrett,Junyi Jessy Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了AstroVisBench，一个用于天文学领域科学计算和可视化的新基准，以评估大型语言模型（LLMs）在科学研究中的应用能力。该基准包含天文学特定工作流的处理和分析数据，以及通过复杂图表可视化结果的能力。研究还引入了一种新颖的“LLM作为裁判”的工作流来评估可视化效果，并通过五位天文学家的标注进行了验证。评估结果显示，目前最先进的LLMs在作为天文学研究助手方面存在显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学研究，特别是天文学，通常需要处理和可视化数据来发现模式并获得新的见解。虽然大型语言模型（LLMs）在文献综合、问答、生成研究想法和进行计算实验方面显示出潜力，但评估LLM介导的科学工作流是否能产生正确的科学见解，尤其是在可视化方面，是一个尚未解决的挑战。这项工作的动机是创建一个专门的基准来解决这个评估难题，从而推动AI在科学发现中的应用。

Method: 研究提出了AstroVisBench，这是第一个专门用于天文学领域科学计算和可视化的基准。该基准包含两部分评估：1）LLM生成天文学特定工作流以处理和分析数据的能力；2）LLM生成复杂图表以可视化这些工作流结果的能力。可视化评估采用了一种新颖的“LLM作为裁判”的方法，该方法通过五位专业天文学家的标注进行了验证，以确保评估的准确性和可靠性。研究使用AstroVisBench对当前最先进的LLMs进行了评估。

Result: 使用AstroVisBench进行的评估显示，尽管LLMs在某些方面有所进展，但它们在有效协助天文学研究方面仍存在显著差距。具体来说，LLMs在生成复杂数据处理工作流和创建准确、信息丰富的天文学可视化图表方面表现不佳。这表明当前的LLMs在理解和执行需要深入领域知识和复杂计算/可视化技能的天文学研究任务方面能力有限。

Conclusion: AstroVisBench的提出填补了在科学计算和可视化领域评估LLM能力的空白，特别是在天文学领域。评估结果揭示了当前LLMs在作为“AI科学家”方面的局限性，尤其是在数据处理和可视化方面。这项工作为开发更强大的、能够支持可视化工作流（这是从物理到生物等广泛领域的核心）的AI科学助手指明了方向，并强调了在天文学等领域进一步发展LLM能力的必要性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are being explored for applications in
scientific research, including their capabilities to synthesize literature,
answer research questions, generate research ideas, and even conduct
computational experiments. Ultimately, our goal is for these to help scientists
derive novel scientific insights. In many areas of science, such insights often
arise from processing and visualizing data to understand its patterns. However,
evaluating whether an LLM-mediated scientific workflow produces outputs
conveying the correct scientific insights is challenging to evaluate and has
not been addressed in past work. We introduce AstroVisBench, the first
benchmark for both scientific computing and visualization in the astronomy
domain. AstroVisBench judges a language model's ability to both (1) create
astronomy-specific workflows to process and analyze data and (2) visualize the
results of these workflows through complex plots. Our evaluation of
visualizations uses a novel LLM-as-a-judge workflow, which is validated against
annotation by five professional astronomers. Using AstroVisBench we present an
evaluation of state-of-the-art language models, showing a significant gap in
their ability to engage in astronomy research as useful assistants. This
evaluation provides a strong end-to-end evaluation for AI scientists that
offers a path forward for the development of visualization-based workflows,
which are central to a broad range of domains from physics to biology.

</details>


### [51] [Accelerating Diffusion LLMs via Adaptive Parallel Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.00413)
*Daniel Israel,Guy Van den Broeck,Aditya Grover*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了解决大型语言模型（LLMs）自回归解码的速度瓶颈，我们提出了自适应并行解码（APD）方法。APD通过结合扩散大型语言模型（dLLMs）的边际概率和小辅助自回归模型的联合概率，动态调整并行采样 token 的数量，从而在理论上实现并行生成。此外，我们通过启用 KV 缓存和限制掩码输入的大小来优化 APD。APD 提供了三个可调参数，允许在吞吐量和质量之间进行灵活权衡，并在下游基准测试中实现了显著更高的吞吐量，同时质量损失极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归解码是大型语言模型（LLMs）生成速度的主要瓶颈，因为它要求逐个按顺序预测 token。虽然扩散大型语言模型（dLLMs）在理论上允许并行生成 token，但在实践中，它们往往难以在不显著牺牲模型质量的情况下达到自回归模型的速度。因此，存在一个迫切需要改进 LLM 生成速度，尤其是在不影响输出质量的情况下。

Method: 我们引入了一种名为自适应并行解码（APD）的新方法。APD 的核心思想是动态地调整并行采样的 token 数量。这通过定义 dLLM 的边际概率和来自一个小型辅助自回归模型（ARM）的序列联合概率之间的乘法混合来实现。这种方法与标准的投机解码（speculative decoding）设置相反，后者旨在通过从小模型草拟（drafting）来从一个大型自回归验证器（verifier）进行采样。为了进一步优化 APD，我们采用了 KV 缓存技术，并限制了掩码输入的规模。APD 提供了三个可调参数，允许用户根据具体需求灵活地在吞吐量和输出质量之间进行权衡。

Result: 实验结果表明，APD 方法在保持极低质量损失的情况下，显著提高了生成吞吐量。在下游基准测试中的评估显示，APD 能够以比现有方法更高的速度生成文本，同时保持了与自回归模型相当的输出质量。

Conclusion: 自适应并行解码（APD）是一种新颖有效的方法，解决了大型语言模型（LLMs）在生成速度方面面临的挑战。通过结合 dLLMs 的并行生成能力和 ARMs 的高效采样机制，APD 实现了在吞吐量和质量之间取得良好的平衡。尽管 APD 在提高效率方面取得了显著成效，但未来的研究可以进一步探索更精细的自适应策略和与其他并行解码技术的集成，以期在不同场景下实现最佳性能。

Abstract: The generation speed of LLMs are bottlenecked by autoregressive decoding,
where tokens are predicted sequentially one by one. Alternatively, diffusion
large language models (dLLMs) theoretically allow for parallel token
generation, but in practice struggle to achieve the speed of autoregressive
models without significantly sacrificing quality. We therefore introduce
adaptive parallel decoding (APD), a novel method that dynamically adjusts the
number of tokens sampled in parallel. We achieve this by defining a
multiplicative mixture between the dLLM marginal probabilities and the joint
probability of sequences under a small auxiliary autoregressive model. This
inverts the standard setup of speculative decoding, where the goal is to sample
from a large autoregressive verifier by drafting from a smaller model. We
further optimize APD by enabling KV caching and limiting the size of the masked
input. Altogether, our method puts forward three tunable parameters to flexibly
tradeoff throughput and quality. We show that APD provides markedly higher
throughput with minimal quality degradations on downstream benchmarks.

</details>


### [52] [FastLongSpeech: Enhancing Large Speech-Language Models for Efficient Long-Speech Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.14815)
*Shoutao Guo,Shaolei Zhang,Qingkai Fang,Zhengrui Ma,Min Zhang,Yang Feng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了FastLongSpeech框架，通过迭代融合策略和动态压缩训练，实现了在无长语音训练数据的情况下，高效处理长语音任务，并提升了长语音和短语音任务的性能及推理效率。同时，开发了长语音理解基准LongSpeech-Eval。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语音语言模型（LSLMs）在长语音处理方面存在挑战，主要是由于缺乏长语音训练数据集和处理长序列的高计算成本。本研究旨在解决这一问题，使LSLMs能够高效处理长语音，而无需专门的长语音训练数据。

Method: FastLongSpeech框架采用迭代融合策略压缩长语音序列至可管理长度。通过动态压缩训练，模型在不同压缩率的短语音序列上进行训练，将短语音能力迁移至长语音任务。此外，研究还开发了一个名为LongSpeech-Eval的长语音理解基准。

Result: 实验证明，FastLongSpeech在长语音和短语音任务上均表现出色，同时显著提高了推理效率。

Conclusion: FastLongSpeech成功解决了长语音处理的效率和数据稀疏性问题，为LSLMs在长语音领域的应用提供了有效解决方案，并在长语音和短语音任务上均取得了优越性能，同时提升了推理效率。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在更多实际场景中的应用。

Abstract: The rapid advancement of Large Language Models (LLMs) has spurred significant
progress in Large Speech-Language Models (LSLMs), enhancing their capabilities
in both speech understanding and generation. While existing LSLMs often
concentrate on augmenting speech generation or tackling a diverse array of
short-speech tasks, the efficient processing of long-form speech remains a
critical yet underexplored challenge. This gap is primarily attributed to the
scarcity of long-speech training datasets and the high computational costs
associated with long sequences. To address these limitations, we introduce
FastLongSpeech, a novel framework designed to extend LSLM capabilities for
efficient long-speech processing without necessitating dedicated long-speech
training data. FastLongSpeech incorporates an iterative fusion strategy that
can compress excessively long-speech sequences into manageable lengths. To
adapt LSLMs for long-speech inputs, it introduces a dynamic compression
training approach, which exposes the model to short-speech sequences at varying
compression ratios, thereby transferring the capabilities of LSLMs to
long-speech tasks. To assess the long-speech capabilities of LSLMs, we develop
a long-speech understanding benchmark called LongSpeech-Eval. Experiments show
that our method exhibits strong performance in both long-speech and
short-speech tasks, while greatly improving inference efficiency.

</details>


### [53] [Curse of Knowledge: When Complex Evaluation Context Benefits yet Biases LLM Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.03419)
*Weiyuan Li,Xintao Wang,Siyu Yuan,Rui Xu,Jiangjie Chen,Qingqing Dong,Yanghua Xiao,Deqing Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了ComplexEval基准，用于评估大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂任务中的可靠性，并发现了LLMs（尤其是大型推理模型LRMs）容易受到辅助信息诱导的偏见影响，偏见程度随任务复杂度增加而加剧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型（LLMs）能力的增强，它们面临的任务日益复杂多样，这使得可靠的评估变得困难。尽管“LLMs作为裁判”的范式提供了一种可扩展的解决方案，但现有研究主要集中在简单场景，对于在需要多方面评分标准、非结构化参考答案和细微判断标准的复杂任务中LLMs作为裁判的可靠性仍有待深入研究。

Method: 研究构建了一个名为ComplexEval的挑战性基准，旨在系统性地暴露和量化辅助信息诱导的偏见。通过在12个基础场景和3个高级场景中，对6种先前未被探索的偏见进行了系统性调查和验证。

Result: 研究发现，所有被评估的模型都显著容易受到这些偏见的影响，且偏见的程度会随着任务复杂度的增加而增强。特别地，大型推理模型（LRMs）表现出一种反常的脆弱性。

Conclusion: 该研究深入分析了LLMs在复杂评估任务中存在的偏见问题，揭示了偏见与任务复杂度之间的关系，并特别指出了大型推理模型（LRMs）的脆弱性。这些发现为了改进评估信号的准确性和可验证性提供了关键见解，为开发更通用、更鲁棒的评估模型奠定了基础。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) grow more capable, they face increasingly
diverse and complex tasks, making reliable evaluation challenging. The paradigm
of LLMs as judges has emerged as a scalable solution, yet prior work primarily
focuses on simple settings. Their reliability in complex tasks--where
multi-faceted rubrics, unstructured reference answers, and nuanced criteria are
critical--remains understudied. In this paper, we constructed ComplexEval, a
challenge benchmark designed to systematically expose and quantify Auxiliary
Information Induced Biases. We systematically investigated and validated 6
previously unexplored biases across 12 basic and 3 advanced scenarios. Key
findings reveal: (1) all evaluated models exhibit significant susceptibility to
these biases, with bias magnitude scaling with task complexity; (2) notably,
Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) show paradoxical vulnerability. Our in-depth
analysis offers crucial insights for improving the accuracy and verifiability
of evaluation signals, paving the way for more general and robust evaluation
models.

### [54] [Ready to Translate, Not to Represent? Bias and Performance Gaps in Multilingual LLMs Across Language Families and Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.07877)
*Md. Faiyaz Abdullah Sayeedi,Md. Mahbub Alam,Subhey Sadi Rahman,Md. Adnanul Islam,Jannatul Ferdous Deepti,Tasnim Mohiuddin,Md Mofijul Islam,Swakkhar Shatabda*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLMs在机器翻译（MT）领域表现出色，但存在跨语言和领域性能不均以及放大训练数据中偏见的问题。为解决这些问题，本文提出了Translation Tangles框架和数据集，用于评估开源LLMs的翻译质量和公平性。该框架在一个包含24种双向语言对和多个领域的数据集上进行基准测试，并采用了一种结合规则启发式、语义相似性过滤和LLM验证的混合偏见检测流程。此外，还引入了一个基于人工评估的、包含1439个翻译-参考对的高质量、偏见标注数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在机器翻译（MT）方面取得了显著进展，但它们在不同语言家族和专业领域之间表现不一，并且可能放大训练数据中的偏见，尤其是在低资源语言中，这引发了对公平性的担忧。因此，需要一个框架来系统地评估LLMs的翻译质量和公平性。

Method: 本文提出了Translation Tangles，一个用于评估开源LLMs翻译质量和公平性的统一框架和数据集。该框架在一个包含24种双向语言对和多个领域的数据集上进行基准测试。偏见检测采用混合方法，结合了规则启发式、语义相似性过滤和LLM验证。此外，构建了一个包含1439个翻译-参考对的高质量、偏见标注数据集，该数据集基于人工评估。

Result: Translation Tangles框架在一个包含24种双向语言对和多个领域的数据集上对开源LLMs进行了基准测试。通过混合偏见检测流程，评估了翻译质量和公平性。人工评估的1439个翻译-参考对构成了一个高质量、偏见标注的数据集，为LLMs的评估提供了依据。

Conclusion: Translation Tangles为评估开源LLMs的翻译质量和公平性提供了一个全面的框架和数据集，解决了现有模型在性能和公平性方面存在的差距。该研究强调了在低资源语言和专业领域中LLMs翻译的潜在偏见问题，并为未来的研究和模型开发指明了方向。代码和数据集已公开（GitHub链接：https://github.com/faiyazabdullah/TranslationTangles）。

Abstract: The rise of Large Language Models (LLMs) has redefined Machine Translation
(MT), enabling context-aware and fluent translations across hundreds of
languages and textual domains. Despite their remarkable capabilities, LLMs
often exhibit uneven performance across language families and specialized
domains. Moreover, recent evidence reveals that these models can encode and
amplify different biases present in their training data, posing serious
concerns for fairness, especially in low-resource languages. To address these
gaps, we introduce Translation Tangles, a unified framework and dataset for
evaluating the translation quality and fairness of open-source LLMs. Our
approach benchmarks 24 bidirectional language pairs across multiple domains
using different metrics. We further propose a hybrid bias detection pipeline
that integrates rule-based heuristics, semantic similarity filtering, and
LLM-based validation. We also introduce a high-quality, bias-annotated dataset
based on human evaluations of 1,439 translation-reference pairs. The code and
dataset are accessible on GitHub:
https://github.com/faiyazabdullah/TranslationTangles

### [55] [Prompt-MII: Meta-Learning Instruction Induction for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.16932)
*Emily Xiao,Yixiao Zeng,Ada Chen,Chin-Jou Li,Amanda Bertsch,Graham Neubig*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出PROMPT-MII，一种基于强化学习的框架，通过“指令归纳”技术，将大量训练样本压缩成简洁的提示，在保持与全数据集相同的性能下，显著减少推理时所需的token数量（3-13倍），解决了LLM in-context learning（ICL）推理成本高的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）的上下文学习（ICL）能力强大，但随着上下文长度增加，推理成本急剧上升。因此，需要一种方法来降低ICL的成本，同时保持其性能。

Method: 本文提出PROMPT-MII框架，利用强化学习（RL）来“归纳”指令。该框架能够为任意新数据集动态生成简洁有效的指令提示。在3000多个HuggingFace数据集上进行训练，并在90个未见过的数据集上进行评估。

Result: PROMPT-MII将下游模型的F1分数提高了4-9个百分点（相对提升10-20%），性能与使用全训练集的ICL相当，但所需的token数量减少了3-13倍。

Conclusion: PROMPT-MII成功地通过指令归纳技术，在保持高性能的同时，大幅降低了LLMs的ICL推理成本，为在实际应用中更高效地利用LLMs提供了有效方案。未来可探索更广泛的应用场景和指令归纳模型的优化。

Abstract: A popular method to adapt large language models (LLMs) to new tasks is
in-context learning (ICL), which is effective but incurs high inference costs
as context length grows. In this paper we propose a method to perform
instruction induction, where we take training examples and reduce them to a
compact but descriptive prompt that can achieve performance comparable to ICL
over the full training set. Specifically, we propose PROMPT-MII, a
reinforcement learning (RL) based framework to meta-learn an instruction
induction model that can generate compact instructions on the fly for an
arbitrary new dataset. We train on over 3,000 diverse classification datasets
from the HuggingFace hub, and evaluate on 90 unseen tasks. PROMPT-MII improves
downstream model quality by 4-9 F1 points (10-20% relative), matching ICL
performance while requiring 3-13x fewer tokens.

</details>


### [56] [Navigating the Alignment-Calibration Trade-off: A Pareto-Superior Frontier via Model Merging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17426)
*Tiancheng Hu,Benjamin Minixhofer,Nigel Collier*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 文章指出，模型对齐（alignment）后通常会出现“对齐税”，这不仅表现为任务准确率下降，还会严重损害模型的校准能力，导致模型过于自信、不可靠且输出多样性降低。研究提出了一种简单的后处理方法——通过插值对齐前后模型的权重，有效缓解了这种权衡。实验发现，这种插值方法能持续找到帕累托最优解，即在提高准确率的同时，还能显著恢复在对齐过程中损失的校准能力。该研究证明，简单的模型合并技术可以高效地减轻对齐税的全部影响，从而得到能力更强、更可靠的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: “对齐税”通常被认为是模型在对齐（alignment）过程中出现的任务准确率下降问题。然而，本文认为“对齐税”的影响更为广泛，除了准确率下降，还会严重损害模型的校准能力，导致模型输出过于自信、可靠性降低，并且多样性不足。这对于期望模型在各种场景下都能提供准确且可靠输出的应用来说，是一个亟待解决的问题。

Method: 本研究提出了一种简单的后处理干预方法，即对齐齐（alignment）前后的模型权重进行插值。具体而言，研究人员不是直接使用对齐后的模型，而是通过线性插值的方式，结合对齐前和对齐后的模型权重，生成一系列新的模型。通过调整插值比例，可以探索不同程度的对齐和原模型能力的结合。

Result: 研究发现，通过对齐前后的模型权重进行插值，可以有效缓解“对齐税”带来的负面影响。具体来说，这种插值方法不仅能够提升模型在任务上的准确率，甚至可以超越对齐前后的“父模型”，同时还能显著恢复在对齐过程中损失的校准能力。实验结果表明，这种方法能够找到帕累托最优解，即在准确率和校准能力之间取得了更好的平衡，而不是简单的权衡。

Conclusion: 本研究成功证明，简单的模型合并（权重插值）技术是一种计算高效且有效的方法，可以减轻“对齐税”带来的全面影响。通过对齐前后的模型权重进行插值，可以获得在准确性和可靠性（校准能力）上都优于单一模型的模型。这为在保证模型能力的同时，提高模型可靠性和输出多样性提供了新的途径，同时也指明了未来模型优化和部署的一个有前景的方向。

Abstract: The "alignment tax" of post-training is typically framed as a drop in task
accuracy. We show it also involves a severe loss of calibration, making models
overconfident, less reliable, and model outputs less diverse. We show that this
trade-off can be navigated effectively via a simple post-hoc intervention:
interpolating between a model's weights before and after alignment. Crucially,
this is not a strict trade-off. We find that the process consistently reveals
Pareto-optimal interpolations - models that improve accuracy beyond both
parents while substantially recovering the calibration lost during alignment.
Our work demonstrates that simple model merging provides a computationally
efficient method for mitigating the full scope of the alignment tax, yielding
models that are more capable and more reliable.

</details>


### [57] [DiffAdapt: Difficulty-Adaptive Reasoning for Token-Efficient LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.19669)
*Xiang Liu,Xuming Hu,Xiaowen Chu,Eunsol Choi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 近期的大型语言模型（LLMs）在解决问题方面表现出色，但其生成的推理过程往往冗长且效率低下。本研究提出了一种名为 DiffAdapt 的轻量级框架，通过分析推理过程中的 token 概率熵，识别并解决了“过度思考”现象。DiffAdapt 能根据问题的难易程度和推理过程的熵特征，为每个问题选择最合适的推理策略（包括提示、温度和最大 token 长度），从而在不进行模型微调的情况下，显著减少 token 使用量，同时保持甚至提高准确性。该方法在多个模型和基准测试上得到了验证，为实现计算高效的推理提供了实际可行的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在解决问题方面展现出强大的能力，但其推理过程（thinking traces）通常非常冗长，这导致了计算资源浪费，并且其有效性尚未得到充分研究。研究的动机在于提高 LLMs 推理的效率，使其在达到高性能的同时避免不必要的“过度思考”，从而在计算成本和性能之间取得更好的平衡。

Method: 本研究首先分析了推理过程中 token 概率的熵。研究人员观察到，在不同难易程度的问题上，熵呈现出一种 U 型模式：简单问题熵高（尽管准确率高），中等难度问题熵低，困难问题熵高（反映了不确定性）。这种模式表明，在简单问题上存在“过度思考”的现象。基于这一洞察，研究者提出了 DiffAdapt 框架。DiffAdapt 使用一个小型探测器（probe）来根据问题的难易程度和推理过程的熵特征，为每个问题选择三种推理策略之一（Easy/Normal/Hard）。每种策略包含固定的提示（prompt）、温度（temperature）和最大 token 长度（maximum token length）。与现有的效率优化方法不同，DiffAdapt 不需要对基础 LLM 进行微调，而是对一个小的探测器进行训练，该探测器可以根据 LLM 的最终隐藏状态进行分类，从而实现低成本的适应性调整。

Result: 研究者在五个模型和八个基准测试上对 DiffAdapt 进行了全面评估。实验结果表明，DiffAdapt 在实现同等或更高准确率的同时，可以将 token 使用量减少高达 22.4%。这证明了 DiffAdapt 在提高 LLM 推理效率方面的有效性，并在计算效率和模型性能之间取得了良好的权衡。

Conclusion: 本研究通过分析推理过程中的熵特征，识别了 LLMs 在处理简单问题时存在的“过度思考”现象，并提出了 DiffAdapt 框架来解决这一问题。DiffAdapt 框架能够根据问题的难易程度和熵特征自适应地选择推理策略，从而在不牺牲准确性的前提下显著降低 token 使用量。该方法成本低廉，易于适应，为实现计算高效的推理提供了一条实际可行的路径。未来的工作可以进一步探索熵特征在理解和优化 LLMs 推理过程中的作用，以及开发更精细的自适应策略。

Abstract: Recent reasoning Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable
problem-solving abilities but often generate long thinking traces whose utility
is unclear. Our work aims to improve their efficiency, enabling them to reach
high performance without overthinking. First, we analyze the entropy of token
probabilities in reasoning traces. Across three models, we observe a consistent
U-shaped entropy pattern: high entropy on easy problems despite high accuracy,
low entropy on problems with medium difficulty, and high entropy on hard
problems reflecting uncertainty. Specifically, we notice 22--25\% entropy
reduction from easy to medium difficulty regions, suggesting an {overthinking}
phenomenon on easy instances. Building on these insights, we introduce
\textbf{DiffAdapt}, a lightweight framework that selects Easy/Normal/Hard
inference strategies per question based on their difficulty and reasoning trace
entropy. Each inference strategy consists of a fixed prompt, temperature and
maximum token length. In contrast to existing efficiency optimization methods,
our approach does not fine-tune base LLM but a small probe that classifies
LLM's final hidden state, allowing inexpensive adaptation. We comprehensively
evaluate our method on five models and eight benchmarks. Our method achieves
comparable or improved accuracy while reducing token usage by up to 22.4\%,
establishing a practical path toward compute-efficient reasoning.

</details>


### [58] [E2Rank: Your Text Embedding can Also be an Effective and Efficient Listwise Reranker](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.22733)
*Qi Liu,Yanzhao Zhang,Mingxin Li,Dingkun Long,Pengjun Xie,Jiaxin Mao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: E2Rank框架通过在现有文本嵌入模型上进行微调，使其能够同时进行高效检索和列表式重排，显著提升了搜索应用的排序保真度，同时保持了高效率。该方法利用查询和候选文档构建“伪查询”，在不牺牲基础嵌入模型性能的前提下，实现了最先进的重排效果，并在多个基准测试中表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文本嵌入模型在搜索应用中虽然效率高且性能可接受，但在排序保真度方面不如专门的重排模型，尤其是在处理细粒度的查询-文档和文档-文档交互方面。特别是基于LLM的列表式重排模型，虽然效果好，但计算成本高。因此，迫切需要一种能够兼顾检索效率和重排精度的统一框架。

Method: E2Rank框架提出了一种通过持续训练来扩展单个文本嵌入模型以同时执行检索和列表式重排的统一方法。具体而言，它利用余弦相似度作为统一的排序函数，并将从原始查询及其候选文档构建的列表式重排提示（prompt）作为增强查询，此过程类似于传统检索模型的伪相关反馈（PRF）。这种方法在保留基础嵌入模型的高效性和表示能力的同时，提升了其重排性能。实验在BEIR重排基准和BRIGHT基准上进行了评估，并与MTEB基准上的嵌入性能进行了比较。

Result: E2Rank在BEIR重排基准上取得了最先进的性能，并在BRIGHT基准上展现了与推理密集型任务相当的性能，同时保持了极低的重排延迟。此外，实验证明该排序训练过程还能提升模型在MTEB基准上的嵌入性能。

Conclusion: 研究表明，单个文本嵌入模型可以通过列表式重排目标进行有效训练，从而统一检索和重排任务，实现计算效率和排序准确性的结合。E2Rank框架为在保持高效率的同时提高搜索应用的排序质量提供了一种有效途径。

Abstract: Text embedding models serve as a fundamental component in real-world search
applications. By mapping queries and documents into a shared embedding space,
they deliver competitive retrieval performance with high efficiency. However,
their ranking fidelity remains limited compared to dedicated rerankers,
especially recent LLM-based listwise rerankers, which capture fine-grained
query-document and document-document interactions. In this paper, we propose a
simple yet effective unified framework E2Rank, means Efficient Embedding-based
Ranking (also means Embedding-to-Rank), which extends a single text embedding
model to perform both high-quality retrieval and listwise reranking through
continued training under a listwise ranking objective, thereby achieving strong
effectiveness with remarkable efficiency. By applying cosine similarity between
the query and document embeddings as a unified ranking function, the listwise
ranking prompt, which is constructed from the original query and its candidate
documents, serves as an enhanced query enriched with signals from the top-K
documents, akin to pseudo-relevance feedback (PRF) in traditional retrieval
models. This design preserves the efficiency and representational quality of
the base embedding model while significantly improving its reranking
performance. Empirically, E2Rank achieves state-of-the-art results on the BEIR
reranking benchmark and demonstrates competitive performance on the
reasoning-intensive BRIGHT benchmark, with very low reranking latency. We also
show that the ranking training process improves embedding performance on the
MTEB benchmark. Our findings indicate that a single embedding model can
effectively unify retrieval and reranking, offering both computational
efficiency and competitive ranking accuracy.

</details>

### [59] [Inverse Knowledge Search over Verifiable Reasoning: Synthesizing a Scientific Encyclopedia from a Long Chains-of-Thought Knowledge Base](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26854)
*Yu Li,Yuan Huang,Tao Wang,Caiyu Fan,Xiansheng Cai,Sihan Hu,Xinzijian Liu,Cheng Shi,Mingjun Xu,Zhen Wang,Yan Wang,Xiangqi Jin,Tianhan Zhang,Linfeng Zhang,Lei Wang,Youjin Deng,Pan Zhang,Weijie Sun,Xingyu Li,Weinan E,Linfeng Zhang,Zhiyuan Yao,Kun Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个名为SciencePedia的可扩展框架，通过“长推理链”（LCoT）知识库解压科学推理，旨在提高科学知识的可验证性和跨领域联系。该框架通过Socratic智能体生成问题，并由多个独立模型生成和验证推理链，最终形成一个包含约200,000个条目的百科全书。评估结果显示，SciencePedia生成的文章在知识点密度和事实准确性方面优于基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学材料通常压缩推理过程，省略了支持结论的推导链，这阻碍了验证并限制了跨领域概念之间的逻辑和因果联系。因此，需要一种能够解压科学推理、建立可验证的推理链并促进知识综合的方法。

Method: 研究提出了一种端点驱动的、还原论的策略。首先，一个Socratic智能体在约200门课程的指导下，生成约300万个第一性原理问题。然后，多个独立的求解模型生成LCoTs，并通过提示清理和跨模型答案共识进行严格筛选，只保留具有可验证端点的推理链。该验证语料库被用于“Brainstorm Search Engine”，该引擎执行逆向知识搜索，检索多样化的、以目标概念为终点的第一性原理推导。最后，Plato合成器将这些验证过的推理链整合成连贯的文章，形成了SciencePedia。初始的SciencePedia包含约200,000个细粒度条目，涵盖数学、物理、化学、生物、工程和计算等学科。

Result: 在跨六个学科的评估中，Plato合成的文章（基于检索到的LCoTs）与未进行检索的基线模型相比，表现出显著更高的知识点密度和更低的事实错误率（由外部LLM评判）。

Conclusion: 该基于推理的方法能够大规模地实现可信赖的、跨领域的科学综合，并为不断扩展的百科全书奠定了基础。它通过解压科学推理，建立了可验证的LCoT知识库，解决了现有科学材料中推理过程不透明的问题。未来的工作可以进一步扩展知识库的范围和深度，并探索更多元的跨领域知识综合应用。

Abstract: Most scientific materials compress reasoning, presenting conclusions while
omitting the derivational chains that justify them. This compression hinders
verification by lacking explicit, step-wise justifications and inhibits
cross-domain links by collapsing the very pathways that establish the logical
and causal connections between concepts. We introduce a scalable framework that
decompresses scientific reasoning, constructing a verifiable Long
Chain-of-Thought (LCoT) knowledge base and projecting it into an emergent
encyclopedia, SciencePedia. Our pipeline operationalizes an endpoint-driven,
reductionist strategy: a Socratic agent, guided by a curriculum of around 200
courses, generates approximately 3 million first-principles questions. To
ensure high fidelity, multiple independent solver models generate LCoTs, which
are then rigorously filtered by prompt sanitization and cross-model answer
consensus, retaining only those with verifiable endpoints. This verified corpus
powers the Brainstorm Search Engine, which performs inverse knowledge search --
retrieving diverse, first-principles derivations that culminate in a target
concept. This engine, in turn, feeds the Plato synthesizer, which narrates
these verified chains into coherent articles. The initial SciencePedia
comprises approximately 200,000 fine-grained entries spanning mathematics,
physics, chemistry, biology, engineering, and computation. In evaluations
across six disciplines, Plato-synthesized articles (conditioned on retrieved
LCoTs) exhibit substantially higher knowledge-point density and significantly
lower factual error rates than an equally-prompted baseline without retrieval
(as judged by an external LLM). Built on this verifiable LCoT knowledge base,
this reasoning-centric approach enables trustworthy, cross-domain scientific
synthesis at scale and establishes the foundation for an ever-expanding
encyclopedia.

</details>


### [60] [The Denario project: Deep knowledge AI agents for scientific discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26887)
*Francisco Villaescusa-Navarro,Boris Bolliet,Pablo Villanueva-Domingo,Adrian E. França,ChangHoon Hahn,Yan-Fei Jiang,Raul Jimenez,Jun-Young Lee,Antonio Lerario,Osman Mamun,Thomas Meier,Anupam A. Ojha,Pavlos Protopapas,Shimanto Roy,David N. Spergel,Pedro Tarancón-Álvarez,Ujjwal Tiwari,Matteo Viel,Digvijay Wadekar,Chi Wang,Bonny Y. Wang,Licong Xu,Yossi Yovel,Shuwen Yue,Wen-Han Zhou,Qiyao Zhu,Jiajun Zou,Íñigo Zubeldia*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Denario是一个AI多智能体系统，旨在作为科学研究助手，能够执行包括生成想法、文献检索、研究计划制定、代码编写与执行、绘图以及论文撰写与审阅在内的多种任务。该系统采用模块化架构，并利用Cmbagent作为深度研究后端，支持端到端的科学分析。论文展示了Denario在天体物理学、生物学、生物物理学、生物医学信息学、化学、材料科学、数学物理、医学、神经科学和行星科学等多个学科生成的AI论文，并特别强调了其跨学科整合能力，例如将量子物理和机器学习方法应用于天体物理数据。通过领域专家的评估（包括评分和评语），论文探讨了Denario的优势、劣势和局限性，并讨论了AI驱动研究的伦理影响及与科学哲学的关系。代码已开源，并提供了在线演示。

Result: Denario成功生成了涵盖多个科学领域的AI论文，并展现了其跨学科整合的能力，例如一篇论文将量子物理和机器学习方法应用于天体物理数据。领域专家的评估结果（包括数值评分和评语）被用于衡量Denario的性能。论文详细分析了Denario在各项任务中的优势、劣势和局限性。

Conclusion: Denario作为一个AI多智能体系统，能够有效地辅助科学研究的多个环节，甚至实现跨学科的创新性研究。尽管目前系统存在局限性，但其潜力巨大，预示着AI在未来科学研究中将扮演越来越重要的角色。论文的发布不仅提供了系统的实现细节和评估结果，还引发了对AI驱动研究的伦理和社会影响的深入思考。

Abstract: We present Denario, an AI multi-agent system designed to serve as a
scientific research assistant. Denario can perform many different tasks, such
as generating ideas, checking the literature, developing research plans,
writing and executing code, making plots, and drafting and reviewing a
scientific paper. The system has a modular architecture, allowing it to handle
specific tasks, such as generating an idea, or carrying out end-to-end
scientific analysis using Cmbagent as a deep-research backend. In this work, we
describe in detail Denario and its modules, and illustrate its capabilities by

technology relates to the philosophy of science. We publicly release the code

Abstract: Cyber-physical systems increasingly rely on Foundational Models such as Large
Language Models (LLMs) and Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to increase autonomy

also introduce new types of errors, such as hallucinations,

### [62] [SUSTAINABLE Platform: Seamless Smart Farming Integration Towards Agronomy Automation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.26989)
*Agorakis Bompotas,Konstantinos Koutras,Nikitas Rigas Kalogeropoulos,Panagiotis Kechagias,Dimitra Gariza,Athanasios P. Kalogeras,Christos Alexakos*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SUSTAINABLE是一个集成了物联网、人工智能、卫星成像和基于角色的任务编排的智慧农业平台，旨在实现高效、可追溯和可持续的农业，并在葡萄栽培领域进行了试点应用。该研究探讨了现有的智慧农业解决方案，进行了比较评估，并介绍了SUSTAINABLE的关键特性，包括卫星指数集成、实时环境数据和针对地中海葡萄园的角色感知任务管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全球农业部门正经历转型，面临日益增长的粮食需求、气候变化和对可持续实践的需求。SUSTAINABLE平台的开发旨在应对这些挑战，提高农业效率、可追溯性和可持续性。

Conclusion: SUSTAINABLE平台通过集成先进技术（物联网、人工智能、卫星成像）和创新的任务管理方法，为应对全球农业挑战提供了一个解决方案，特别是在葡萄栽培领域。该研究强调了该平台在提高农业效率、可追溯性和可持续性方面的潜力。

Abstract: The global agricultural sector is undergoing a transformative shift, driven
by increasing food demands, climate variability and the need for sustainable
practices. SUSTAINABLE is a smart farming platform designed to integrate IoT,
AI, satellite imaging, and role-based task orchestration to enable efficient,
traceable, and sustainable agriculture with a pilot usecase in viticulture.

evaluation, and introduces SUSTAINABLE's key features, including satellite
index integration, real-time environmental data, and role-aware task management
tailored to Mediterranean vineyards.

### [63] [Causal Masking on Spatial Data: An Information-Theoretic Case for Learning Spatial Datasets with Unimodal Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27009)
*Jared Junkin,Samuel Nathanson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 在非序列数据（如棋盘）上，因果掩码（causal masking）被认为不适合，通常使用顺序线性化。本研究在国际象棋领域，该领域同时支持空间（棋盘）和顺序（走子）表示，探究了因果掩码的信息损失是否可行。实验证明，即使使用因果掩码，在空间棋盘状态上训练的模型也比在顺序数据上训练的模型具有更强的棋力。这表明因果掩码可用于空间数据训练单模态大语言模型，甚至优于顺序化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统语言模型主要围绕因果掩码设计。然而，在具有空间或关系结构的数据域中，因果掩码常被认为不适用，人们倾向于使用顺序线性化。尽管如此，关于因果掩码在非序列数据上引入的信息损失是否可行的研究却很少。这主要是因为缺乏同时具备空间和顺序表示的数据集。本研究旨在弥合这一知识空白，特别是在国际象棋这一天然支持两种表示方式的领域。

Method: 本研究采用国际象棋作为实验平台，该平台既有空间上的棋盘表示，也有顺序上的走子序列表示。研究人员训练了使用双向和因果自注意力机制的语言模型，分别在空间棋盘状态数据和顺序走子数据上进行训练。实验对比了这两种不同数据表示和注意力机制组合下的模型性能。

Result: 实验结果显示，在空间棋盘状态上训练的模型，即使采用了因果掩码，其棋力表现也始终优于在顺序数据上训练的模型。这表明在处理具有空间结构的数据时，因果掩码并非不可行，并且可能比顺序化方法带来更好的性能。

Conclusion: 本研究在国际象棋领域进行了实验，证明了在空间数据上应用因果掩码是一种可行的训练单模态大语言模型的方法。更重要的是，在某些领域，这种方法甚至优于传统的顺序化方法。尽管实验集中在国际象棋，但其方法学上的意义可能具有更广泛的应用前景，为处理其他具有空间结构的数据提供了新的思路。未来的工作可以探索将此方法扩展到其他领域，并进一步研究因果掩码在不同空间数据结构上的表现。

Abstract: Language models are traditionally designed around causal masking. In domains
with spatial or relational structure, causal masking is often viewed as
inappropriate, and sequential linearizations are instead used. Yet the question
of whether it is viable to accept the information loss introduced by causal
masking on nonsequential data has received little direct study, in part because
few domains offer both spatial and sequential representations of the same
dataset. In this work, we investigate this issue in the domain of chess, which
naturally supports both representations. We train language models with
bidirectional and causal self-attention mechanisms on both spatial
(board-based) and sequential (move-based) data. Our results show that models
trained on spatial board states - \textit{even with causal masking} -
consistently achieve stronger playing strength than models trained on
sequential data. While our experiments are conducted on chess, our results are
methodological and may have broader implications: applying causal masking to
spatial data is a viable procedure for training unimodal LLMs on spatial data,
and in some domains is even preferable to sequentialization.

### [64] [e1: Learning Adaptive Control of Reasoning Effort](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27042)
*Michael Kleinman,Matthew Trager,Alessandro Achille,Wei Xia,Stefano Soatto*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: The paper introduces Adaptive Effort Control (AEC), a self-adaptive reinforcement learning method that allows AI models to dynamically adjust their reasoning effort based on user-specified fractions of the average chain-of-thought length. This approach improves the cost-accuracy tradeoff by eliminating the need for users to pre-determine query difficulty and token budgets. AEC reduces chain-of-thought length by approximately 3x across various model scales while maintaining or improving performance.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing methods for controlling AI model reasoning effort require users to specify absolute token budgets, which necessitates prior knowledge of query difficulty. This is often impractical, leading to suboptimal trade-offs between output quality, latency, and cost. The paper addresses the need for a more flexible and intuitive way for users to control the reasoning "thinking budget" of AI models, allowing them to dynamically balance desired output quality against computational expenses.

Method: The paper proposes Adaptive Effort Control (AEC), a reinforcement learning approach. AEC trains models to utilize a user-specified fraction of tokens relative to the current average chain-of-thought length for each query. This self-adaptive method learns to allocate resources proportionally to task difficulty without requiring dataset- or phase-specific tuning. Users can adjust the cost-accuracy trade-off at inference time using a continuous "effort" parameter.

Result: Experiments across model scales from 1.5B to 32B parameters demonstrate that AEC enables an approximate 3x reduction in chain-of-thought length while preserving or enhancing performance compared to the base model used for reinforcement learning training. The approach yields better cost-accuracy tradeoff curves than standard methods.

Conclusion: Adaptive Effort Control (AEC) offers a novel and effective way for users to dynamically manage the cost-accuracy trade-off in AI models. By allowing fine-grained control over reasoning effort relative to query difficulty, AEC improves efficiency and performance. Future work could explore extending AEC to other generative tasks or investigating more sophisticated methods for determining the optimal effort fraction.

Abstract: Increasing the thinking budget of AI models can significantly improve
accuracy, but not all questions warrant the same amount of reasoning. Users may
prefer to allocate different amounts of reasoning effort depending on how they
value output quality versus latency and cost. To leverage this tradeoff
effectively, users need fine-grained control over the amount of thinking used
for a particular query, but few approaches enable such control. Existing
methods require users to specify the absolute number of desired tokens, but
this requires knowing the difficulty of the problem beforehand to appropriately
set the token budget for a query. To address these issues, we propose Adaptive
Effort Control, a self-adaptive reinforcement learning method that trains
models to use a user-specified fraction of tokens relative to the current
average chain-of-thought length for each query. This approach eliminates
dataset- and phase-specific tuning while producing better cost-accuracy
tradeoff curves compared to standard methods. Users can dynamically adjust the
cost-accuracy trade-off through a continuous effort parameter specified at
inference time. We observe that the model automatically learns to allocate
resources proportionally to the task difficulty and, across model scales
ranging from 1.5B to 32B parameters, our approach enables approximately 3x
reduction in chain-of-thought length while maintaining or improving performance
relative to the base model used for RL training.

### [65] [Fints: Efficient Inference-Time Personalization for LLMs with Fine-Grained Instance-Tailored Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27206)
*Kounianhua Du,Jianxing Liu,Kangning Zhang,Wenxiang Jiao,Yuan Lu,Jiarui Jin,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为Fints的细粒度、实例定制的个性化LLM适应框架，通过动态生成样本级干预向量注入模型的前向传播，以解决现有参数化方法在动态用户模式和数据稀疏场景下的局限性。Fints通过钩取注意力层和MLP层的激活来捕捉细微信号，并利用输入感知聚合模块合成上下文相关的增强，实现了高灵活性和数据效率，在快速变化的分布和高数据稀疏场景下表现优异，且可作为插件兼容现有方法，并在文本生成和函数调用等任务中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展带来了对有效个性化技术的需求，以适应个体用户偏好。尽管存在利用LLM的上下文学习能力的非参数方法，但近期的参数化方法（如个性化参数高效微调和奖励建模）在处理动态用户模式和数据稀疏场景时面临低适应性和数据效率的挑战。因此，需要一种能够克服这些限制的更优的个性化方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种细粒度、实例定制的个性化LLM适应框架，称为Fints。该框架通过两个关键技术创新实现：1. 细粒度转向组件：通过钩取注意力（attention）和多层感知机（MLP）层的激活来捕捉用户数据的细微信号。2. 输入感知聚合模块：将捕捉到的细微信号合成为与上下文相关的增强。这些信号被动态地转化为样本级的干预向量，并注入到模型的正向传播过程中，从而实现个性化适应。实验在短文本到长文本生成以及Web函数调用等多种场景下进行，以验证其有效性和兼容性。

Result: Fints框架在快速变化的分布和高数据稀疏场景下表现出高灵活性和数据效率。在短文本到长文本生成以及Web函数调用等多样化场景的广泛实验中，验证了该方法的有效性和兼容性。实验结果表明，Fints显著提升了在快速变化环境下的个性化性能，并保持了在不同交互模式和上下文长度下的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: Fints框架通过其细粒度的转向组件和输入感知的聚合模块，成功地解决了现有参数化个性化方法在动态用户模式和数据稀疏场景下的局限性。该方法具有高灵活性、数据效率和与现有技术正交的优点，可作为插件集成到不同的个性化技术中。实验证明了Fints在多种场景下的有效性和鲁棒性，为LLM的个性化适应提供了有前景的方向。未来的工作可以探索Fints在更多样化的下游任务中的应用，并进一步优化其计算效率。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of large language models (LLMs) has intensified the
demand for effective personalization techniques that can adapt model behavior
to individual user preferences. Despite the non-parametric methods utilizing
the in-context learning ability of LLMs, recent parametric adaptation methods,
including personalized parameter-efficient fine-tuning and reward modeling
emerge. However, these methods face limitations in handling dynamic user
patterns and high data sparsity scenarios, due to low adaptability and data
efficiency. To address these challenges, we propose a fine-grained and
instance-tailored steering framework that dynamically generates sample-level
interference vectors from user data and injects them into the model's forward
pass for personalized adaptation. Our approach introduces two key technical
innovations: a fine-grained steering component that captures nuanced signals by
hooking activations from attention and MLP layers, and an input-aware
aggregation module that synthesizes these signals into contextually relevant
enhancements. The method demonstrates high flexibility and data efficiency,
excelling in fast-changing distribution and high data sparsity scenarios. In
addition, the proposed method is orthogonal to existing methods and operates as
a plug-in component compatible with different personalization techniques.
Extensive experiments across diverse scenarios--including short-to-long text
generation, and web function calling--validate the effectiveness and
compatibility of our approach. Results show that our method significantly
enhances personalization performance in fast-shifting environments while
maintaining robustness across varying interaction modes and context lengths.
Implementation is available at https://github.com/KounianhuaDu/Fints.

### [66] [Reinforcement Learning for Long-Horizon Unordered Tasks: From Boolean to Coupled Reward Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27329)
*Kristina Levina,Nikolaos Pappas,Athanasios Karapantelakis,Aneta Vulgarakis Feljan,Jendrik Seipp*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出并解决了现有奖励机器（RM）在处理长时序、无序子任务的复杂强化学习问题时的扩展性瓶颈。通过引入数值RM、议程RM和耦合RM三种泛化形式，以及一种基于耦合RM的组合式学习算法CoRM（coupled RM），显著提高了智能体在这些复杂任务中的学习效率和可扩展性。实验证明，CoRM相比于现有的RM算法，在长时序问题上表现出更好的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的奖励机器（RM）在为强化学习（RL）智能体提供环境奖励结构信息方面非常有效，尤其是在处理复杂的非马尔可夫任务时，能够显著提高学习效率并减少样本需求。然而，当面临长时序问题，特别是那些涉及可按任意顺序执行的子任务集时，RM的学习效率会急剧下降。这是因为随着无序子任务数量的增加，需要学习的信息量呈指数级增长，使得现有RM方法难以应对。因此，解决RM在长时序、无序子任务问题上的扩展性瓶颈具有重要意义。

Method: 为了解决上述限制，本研究提出了三种对RM的泛化：1. 数值RM（Numeric RMs）：允许用户以更紧凑的形式表达复杂的任务。2. 议程RM（Agenda RMs）：将状态与一个跟踪待完成子任务的议程相关联。3. 耦合RM（Coupled RMs）：将状态与议程中每个子任务关联的耦合状态相关联。在此基础上，研究引入了一种新的组合式学习算法——与耦合RM相结合的Q学习（CoRM），该算法利用耦合RM的结构来提升学习效率。实验中，通过在长时序、无序子任务问题上进行测试，将CoRM与现有最先进的RM算法进行性能比较。

Result: 实验结果表明，新提出的组合式学习算法CoRM在处理长时序、无序子任务的问题时，相比于现有的基于奖励机器（RM）的算法，展现出了更好的可扩展性。具体来说，CoRM能够更有效地学习和适应这些复杂任务，证明了其泛化RM和组合式学习方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究通过引入数值RM、议程RM和耦合RM，以及基于耦合RM的Q学习算法CoRM，成功地解决了传统RM在处理长时序、无序子任务问题时的扩展性限制。CoRM在实验中表现出优越的可扩展性，为强化学习在复杂任务场景下的应用提供了新的解决方案。未来的工作可以进一步探索这些泛化RM在更多类型的复杂任务中的应用，并研究更高效的组合式学习策略。

Abstract: Reward machines (RMs) inform reinforcement learning agents about the reward
structure of the environment. This is particularly advantageous for complex
non-Markovian tasks because agents with access to RMs can learn more
efficiently from fewer samples. However, learning with RMs is ill-suited for
long-horizon problems in which a set of subtasks can be executed in any order.
In such cases, the amount of information to learn increases exponentially with
the number of unordered subtasks. In this work, we address this limitation by
introducing three generalisations of RMs: (1) Numeric RMs allow users to
express complex tasks in a compact form. (2) In Agenda RMs, states are
associated with an agenda that tracks the remaining subtasks to complete. (3)
Coupled RMs have coupled states associated with each subtask in the agenda.
Furthermore, we introduce a new compositional learning algorithm that leverages
coupled RMs: Q-learning with coupled RMs (CoRM). Our experiments show that CoRM
scales better than state-of-the-art RM algorithms for long-horizon problems
with unordered subtasks.

### [67] [Discriminative Rule Learning for Outcome-Guided Process Model Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27343)
*Ali Norouzifar,Wil van der Aalst*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在事件日志中区分期望与非期望行为，并分别进行过程发现的方法，以生成更具可解释性和面向结果的过程模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的过程发现技术在处理包含期望和非期望执行路径的事件日志时，往往会生成概括性过强的模型，无法有效支持合规性检查和性能分析。简单地聚合所有行为会掩盖导致不同结果的关键结构差异，而仅关注一种行为则可能忽略另一种行为的重要信息。因此，需要一种能够区分不同行为模式并分别建模的方法，以揭示影响过程结果的驱动因素。

Method: 该研究提出了一种基于可解释的判别规则的方法。首先，通过学习控制流特征上的判别规则来区分期望和非期望的事件日志轨迹。然后，根据这些规则将轨迹分组。最后，在每个分组内独立应用过程发现技术，为每种类型的行为生成专门的过程模型。该方法已实现为一个公开可用的工具。

Result: 通过在多个真实世界的事件日志上进行评估，该方法有效地分离和可视化了关键的过程模式。实验表明，该方法能够生成针对特定行为（期望或非期望）的、更具可解释性的过程模型，从而更好地揭示了导致不同过程结果的驱动因素。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的面向结果的过程发现方法，通过区分和分别建模期望与非期望行为，能够生成更精细、更具可解释性的过程模型。这对于理解和优化业务流程，特别是识别和解决导致低效或违规行为的根本原因，具有重要的实际意义。未来的工作可以探索更复杂的特征提取和规则学习方法，以及将该方法应用于更广泛的业务场景。

Abstract: Event logs extracted from information systems offer a rich foundation for
understanding and improving business processes. In many real-world
applications, it is possible to distinguish between desirable and undesirable
process executions, where desirable traces reflect efficient or compliant
behavior, and undesirable ones may involve inefficiencies, rule violations,
delays, or resource waste. This distinction presents an opportunity to guide
process discovery in a more outcome-aware manner. Discovering a single process
model without considering outcomes can yield representations poorly suited for
conformance checking and performance analysis, as they fail to capture critical
behavioral differences. Moreover, prioritizing one behavior over the other may
obscure structural distinctions vital for understanding process outcomes. By
learning interpretable discriminative rules over control-flow features, we
group traces with similar desirability profiles and apply process discovery
separately within each group. This results in focused and interpretable models
that reveal the drivers of both desirable and undesirable executions. The
approach is implemented as a publicly available tool and it is evaluated on
multiple real-life event logs, demonstrating its effectiveness in isolating and
visualizing critical process patterns.

### [68] [An In-depth Study of LLM Contributions to the Bin Packing Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.27353)

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
